<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-size: 10pt"></span></p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; width: 100%"><tr style="vertical-align: top; text-align: justify">
<td style="width: 0%"></td><td style="width: 0.7in; text-align: left"><span style="font-size: 10pt"><b>Item 8.01.</b></span></td><td style="text-align: justify; width: 90%"><span style="font-size: 10pt"><b>Other Events.</b></span></td>
</tr></table>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">On May 20, 2021 (the &#8220;Redemption Date&#8221;), The Coca-Cola Company (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) redeemed all of the outstanding
(i) $423,083,000 aggregate principal amount of the Company&#8217;s 2.950% Notes due 2025 (the &#8220;2.950% Notes&#8221;), (ii) $280,467,000
aggregate principal amount of the Company&#8217;s 2.550% Notes due 2026 (the &#8220;2.550% Notes&#8221;) and (iii) $455,759,000 aggregate
principal amount of the Company&#8217;s 2.250% Notes due 2026 (the &#8220;2.250% Notes&#8221; and, together with the 2.950% Notes and
the 2.550% Notes, the &#8220;Notes&#8221;), under the Amended and Restated Indenture, dated as of April 26, 1988, as amended by the First
Supplemental Indenture, dated as of February 24, 1992, and the Second Supplemental Indenture, dated as of November 1, 2007, between the
Company and Deutsche Bank Trust Company Americas, as trustee.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">The Notes were redeemed at a redemption price of 100% of the principal
amount of the applicable Notes, plus accrued and unpaid interest to, but excluding, the Redemption Date plus the applicable &#8220;make-whole&#8221;
premium.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>
